Solozeroth adds new objects to the database. The new entry/ID numbers start here:  

`creature_template`.`entry` = 251001
`page_text`.`ID` = 4001 (skip 5 between books to easily allow for extra pages in the future)

`item_template`.`entry`: 
To have a new item display properly, the client needs to 'jibe' with the info on the server. 
A simple way to do that is to use some of the unused items that the client already knows about. 
Below is a list of all available items. I have prepended the ones I have used with 
USED(<short description of the new item>) for easy lookups.

List created by Rochet2
Updated list for TC TDB at: http://pastebin.com/hyNUYtMj
Note: Usability in combat of all Consumbables is decided by the spell assigned.
